CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crop (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), growing_season VARCHAR(50), yield_per_acre FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS farmer (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), age INT, gender VARCHAR(10), phone_number VARCHAR(15))

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS machinery (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), condition VARCHAR(50))</t><stat>UPSERT INTO crop (id, name, type, growing_season, yield_per_acre) VALUES (1, 'Crop A', 'Type A', 'Season A', 50.5) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE name = 'Crop A', type = 'Type A', growing_season = 'Season A', yield_per_acre = 50.5</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crop (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), growing_season VARCHAR(50), yield_per_acre FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS machinery (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), condition VARCHAR(50))</t><stat>UPSERT INTO crop (id, name, type, growing_season, yield_per_acre) VALUES (1, 'Crop A', 'Type A', 'Season A', 50.5) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE name = 'Crop A', type = 'Type A', growing_season = 'Season A', yield_per_acre = 50.5</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS field (id INT PRIMARY KEY, farm_id INT, size FLOAT, soil_type VARCHAR(50), FOREIGN KEY (farm_id) REFERENCES farm(id) ON DELETE CASCADE)

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS field (id INT PRIMARY KEY, farm_id INT, size FLOAT, soil_type VARCHAR(50), FOREIGN KEY (farm_id) REFERENCES farm(id) ON DELETE CASCADE)

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crop (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), growing_season VARCHAR(50), yield_per_acre FLOAT)
